NEXT:
  current progress  
  The Dockerfile is based on ubuntu:20.04 with environment and path variables set for amd64 Linux. It attempts to install Python 3.12 and 3.10 packages including venv and distutils via apt-get, but the build fails due to missing packages python3.12-venv, python3.12-distutils, python3.10-venv, and python3.10-distutils which are not found in Ubuntu 20.04 repositories. Other tools such as Go 1.20.7, Kind v0.20.0, gocovmerge, kubectl, Helm, Ansible, and Python dependencies are installed or planned to be installed after the Python setup. The Dockerfile includes user creation, copying of source files, and building the project libraries.
  next step  
  Modify the Dockerfile to correctly install Python 3.12 and Python 3.10 without relying on non-existent apt packages for venv and distutils on Ubuntu 20.04. Options include:  
  - Use deadsnakes PPA or another reliable source to install Python 3.10 and 3.12 with venv and distutils support.  
  - Alternatively, build Python 3.12 and 3.10 from source or use official Python installers for amd64 Linux.  
  - Ensure all required Python components (venv, distutils) are available post-installation.  
  - Adjust the apt-get install command to exclude python3.12-venv and similar packages if installing via other methods.  
  - Verify Python versions and venv/distutils availability before continuing with pip upgrades and further installs.  
  - After fixing Python installation, reattempt building the Docker image.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      software-properties-common \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-distutils python3-pip python3-setuptools \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Upgrade pip for python3.12
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #7 29.12 ===========

  #7 29.12 Reporting Issues
  #7 29.12 ================
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 29.12 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 29.12 ====================================
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 29.12 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 29.12 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 29.12 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 29.12 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 29.12 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 29.12 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Packages
  #7 29.12 ========
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 29.12 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 29.12 ==========================
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 29.12 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 29.12 
  #7 29.12 Sources
  #7 29.12 =======
  #7 29.12 The package sources are available at:
  #7 29.12 https://github.com/deadsnakes/

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update \
      && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-distutils python3.12-dev python3.12-lib2to3 python3-pip python3-setuptools \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Upgrade pip for python3.12
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #7 28.98 Reporting Issues
  #7 28.98 ================
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 28.98 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 28.98 ====================================
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 28.98 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 28.98 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 28.98 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 28.98 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 28.98 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 28.98 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Packages
  #7 28.98 ========
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 28.98 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 28.98 ==========================
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 28.98 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 28.98 
  #7 28.98 Sources
  #7 28.98 =======
  #7 28.98 The package sources are available at:
  #7 28.98 https://github.com/deadsnakes/
  #7 28.98

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update \
      && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3-pip python3-setuptools \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install distutils for python3.12 via pip
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir setuptools
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Upgrade pip for python3.12
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

  #7 29.32  This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Update Note
  #7 29.32 ===========
  #7 29.32 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Reporting Issues
  #7 29.32 ================
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 29.32 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 29.32 ====================================
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 29.32 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 29.32 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 29.32 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 29.32 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 29.32 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 29.32 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Packages
  #7 29.32 ========
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 29.32 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 29.32 ==========================
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 29.32 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 29.32 
  #7 29.32 Sources
  #7 29.32 =======
  #7 29.32 The package sources are available at:
  #7 29.32 https://github.com/deadsnakes/

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update \
      && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3.12-distutils python3-pip python3-setuptools \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Upgrade pip for python3.12
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

PLAN:
  === ADJUSTED ENVIRONMENT SETUP PLAN ===
  **Note:** This plan is adjusted to your hardware context: x86_64 architecture (amd64 Linux), no GPU present, Docker version 28.3.2, working directory `/home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto`, and standard Linux amd64 base images. All instructions and tooling are aligned accordingly.
  ---
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:  
     - **Docker**  
       - Use latest stable Docker version (you have 28.3.2 installed, which supports BuildKit and modern features).  
       - Use amd64 Linux base images only (e.g., `ubuntu:20.04`, `debian:stable-amd64`, `alpine:3.18-amd64`). Avoid ARM or other architectures.  
       - No GPU or CUDA images are needed or applicable due to absence of NVIDIA GPU.  
       - Verify with:  
         ```bash  
         docker --version  
         docker run --platform=linux/amd64 hello-world  
         ```  
       - Use `--platform=linux/amd64` explicitly in Docker commands if multi-arch images are encountered to ensure amd64 images are selected.  
     - **Golang**  
       - Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux.  
       - Use official Go installers or package manager binaries built for amd64 Linux.  
       - Set `GOPATH` and ensure `$GOPATH/bin` is in your PATH.  
       - Install Kind v0.20.0 via:  
         ```bash  
         GOARCH=amd64 GOOS=linux go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0  
         ```  
         or simply:  
         ```bash  
         go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0  
         ```  
         since your host is amd64 Linux.  
       - Verify with: `kind version`  
     - **Kind (Kubernetes in Docker)**  
       - Use version v0.20.0 as specified.  
       - Ensure Kind binary is accessible in PATH (`$GOPATH/bin` or `/usr/local/bin`).  
     - **Python**  
       - Runtime requires Python 3.12+ (amd64 Linux binaries).  
       - Development environment requires at least Python 3.10+.  
       - On older systems (e.g., Ubuntu 20.04 with Python 3.8), manually install Python 3.10+ for dev environment.  
       - Use system package manager or official Python amd64 Linux installers.  
       - Verify with `python3 --version` or inside virtual environment.  
     - **Python dependencies**  
       - Use pinned `requirements.txt` and `requirements-dev.txt` generated with Python 3.12+ on amd64 Linux.  
       - Use `pip-compile` from `pip-tools` installed inside Python 3.12+ venv or system environment.  
       - Development tooling includes black, isort, pylint, mypy (optional), pre-commit, etc.  
       - Ensure all wheels and binary dependencies are compatible with amd64 Linux.  
     - **kubectl**  
       - Install latest stable kubectl client for amd64 Linux.  
       - Verify with `kubectl version --client`  
     - **Helm (optional)**  
       - Use Helm binaries for amd64 Linux if deploying operators with Helm charts.  
       - Verify with `helm version`

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update \
      && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3-pip python3-setuptools \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Upgrade pip for python3.12
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #7 28.22 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 28.22 ====================================
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 28.22 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 28.22 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 28.22 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 28.22 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 28.22 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 28.22 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 Packages
  #7 28.22 ========
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 28.22 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 28.22 ==========================
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 28.22 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 28.22 
  #7 28.22 Sources
  #7 28.22 =======
  #7 28.22 The package sources are available at:
  #7 28.22 https://github.com/deadsnakes/
  #7 28.22

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update \
      && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3.12-distutils \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-distutils python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install system dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3.12-distutils \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #7 22.48 Description:
  #7 22.48 This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Update Note
  #7 22.48 ===========
  #7 22.48 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Reporting Issues
  #7 22.48 ================
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 22.48 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 22.48 ====================================
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 22.48 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 22.48 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 22.48 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 22.48 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 22.48 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 22.48 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Packages
  #7 22.48 ========
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 22.48 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 22.48 ==========================
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 22.48 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 22.48 
  #7 22.48 Sources
  #7 22.48 =======
  #7 22.48 The package sources are available at:
  #7 22.48 https://github.com/deadsnakes/

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 packages from deadsnakes PPA
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3.12-distutils \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev python3.10-lib2to3 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 8 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA (removed python3.12-distutils and python3.10-lib2to3)
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel, and install distutils via pip
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir distutils
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA, including python3.12-distutils
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev python3.12-distutils \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA, excluding python3.12-distutils
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible and required collections in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible==2.17.5 \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA, excluding python3.12-distutils
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible core and required collections in python3.12 environment, without specifying ansible==2.17.5
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      ansible-posix==1.5.0 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 12 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA, excluding python3.12-distutils
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible core and required collections in python3.12 environment, remove ansible-posix from pip install, install collections with ansible-galaxy
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      community.general==6.11.0 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools \
      && ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV GOPATH=/go
  ENV PATH=$GOPATH/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12 packages
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common curl ca-certificates gnupg lsb-release \
   && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
   && apt-get update
  # Install system dependencies and tools including python3.12 and python3.10 packages from deadsnakes PPA, excluding python3.12-distutils
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      unzip \
      make \
      sudo \
      iproute2 \
      iputils-ping \
      netcat \
      bash-completion \
      procps \
      jq \
      python3.12 python3.12-venv python3.12-dev \
      python3.10 python3.10-venv python3.10-dev \
      python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.12 explicitly using ensurepip and upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN python3.12 -m ensurepip --upgrade \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Set python3 to python3.12 explicitly and update alternatives
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.12 2 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1 \
   && update-alternatives --set python3 /usr/bin/python3.12
  # Install Go 1.20+ (latest stable) for amd64 Linux
  ENV GO_VERSION=1.20.7
  RUN curl -fsSL https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz -o go.tar.gz \
   && tar -C /usr/local -xzf go.tar.gz \
   && rm go.tar.gz
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  # Create GOPATH directories
  RUN mkdir -p $GOPATH/{bin,src,pkg}
  # Install Kind v0.20.0 amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install sigs.k8s.io/kind@v0.20.0
  # Install gocovmerge amd64 Linux binary via Go install
  RUN go install github.com/wadey/gocovmerge@latest
  # Install kubectl latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN curl -fsSL -o /usr/local/bin/kubectl https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl \
   && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/kubectl
  # Install Helm latest stable amd64 Linux binary
  RUN HELM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/helm/helm/releases/latest | grep '"tag_name":' | sed -E 's/.*"([^"]+)".*/\1/') \
   && curl -fsSL -o helm.tar.gz https://get.helm.sh/helm-${HELM_VERSION}-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
   && tar -xzf helm.tar.gz --strip-components=1 linux-amd64/helm -C /usr/local/bin/ \
   && rm helm.tar.gz
  # Install Ansible core and required Python packages in python3.12 environment
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
      ansible-core==2.17.5 \
      pre-commit \
      black \
      isort \
      pylint \
      mypy \
      pip-tools
  # Install Ansible collections via ansible-galaxy
  RUN ansible-galaxy collection install ansible.posix community.general
  # Copy repository files to container
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  # Install Python dependencies pinned with requirements.txt and requirements-dev.txt using python3.12
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt \
   && python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt
  # Install pre-commit hooks
  RUN pre-commit install
  # Build the Acto libraries using Makefile
  RUN make lib
  # Set user to cc (create user cc with home directory and sudo)
  RUN useradd -m -d /home/cc -s /bin/bash cc \
   && echo "cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/acto
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/go/bin:/usr/local/go/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
